Usage:\n   logcat [filters]\n\nIf logcat is called with no filter argument, then it displays all\ninstrumentation points of verbose or higher severity.\n\nArguments to logcat provide filters of instrumentation points to display,\nbased on module name, tag and severity. The format of the arguements are a\ncomma or space delimited string with each item containing a colon-delimited\nmodule, tag, and severity\n\nlogcat module:tag:severity module:tag:severity\n\nThe tag and severity items are optional. If the tag item is omitted all\ntags for the module will be associated. If the severity is ommitted a\nseverity of DBG_SEV_H and higher will be associated.\n\nSeverity is expected as:\n\nH - Log high frequency severity and above (H, V, D, I, W, E, F)\nV - Log verbose severity and above (V, D, I, W, E, F)\nD - Log debug severity and above (D, I, W, E, F)\nI - Log informational severity and above (I, W, E, F)\nW - Log warning severity and above (W, E, F)\nE - Log error severity and above (E, F)\nF - Log fatal severity only (F)\n\nExamples:\n\nlogcat FOO:BAR:W,FOO2::D,FOO3\nlogcat FOO FOO2 FOO3::W\nlogcat\n\n
